Foreign Important Telegrams

Hoover Opposes Cancellation of War Debts

Britain and France Consult the United States to Comprehensively Reorganize War Debts

Suspend Payment of Due Installments During Discussion Period

Hoover Indicates Only Conditional Reductions Can Be Made

▲ The National Society reported on the 13th that President Hoover had telegraphed from his special train to President-elect Roosevelt and his advisors, inviting them to jointly discuss the British and French dispatches requesting the suspension of war debt payments on Saturday. At the same time, Hoover told reporters that he personally opposed canceling war debts and believed that debt reduction must be exchanged for commercial benefits. Furthermore, the United States had previously proposed that when negotiating with debtor nations, it was not necessary to limit the discussion to war debts but should also include issues such as global economic stability and disarmament. Hoover expressed strong agreement with the British diplomatic note, which stated that the United States and other major powers were now facing a very important global problem that needed to be resolved urgently and that discussions should not be restricted. He also stated that although the war debt agreement stipulated that debtor nations should notify three months in advance if they wished to postpone payments, Germany had been accommodated previously in October, so accommodation could also be made this time. Therefore, the installments due on December 15th could be postponed, and the British and French request for renewed discussions could also be granted. There were currently no doubts, and it was expected that all debtor nations would make similar requests. Hoover also stated that the United States should accept any proposal to exchange war debts for economic benefits, but such proposals should be made by the debtor nations. The United States would offer a proposal to continue reducing military spending as part of the compensation for reducing or modifying the terms of war debts. In addition, it was reported that the United States would negotiate separately with each debtor nation, starting with the United Kingdom. Once the United Kingdom and the United States had reached an agreement, it would be easier to negotiate with other countries. It was also said that the British and French dispatches contained similar content.

Content of the British and French Notes

▲ Reuters reported from London on the 13th that the British and French official documents regarding war debts to the United States were released today. At the same time, Washington also transmitted the news that President Hoover had asked President-elect Roosevelt to discuss this issue. The British diplomatic note mentioned the agreement to cease various reparations payments in Lausanne, stating that this was the greatest contribution of the governments concerned to the early restoration of global prosperity. The United Kingdom and the United States have a similar deep interest in the restoration of prosperity, and it will not be possible to achieve this without the cooperation of the United States. The British government believes that the current state of financial obligations between governments must be reconsidered and that it is necessary to handle it quickly. The government sincerely hopes that the US government can find ways to exchange views as soon as possible, but the immediate goal of the British government is more limited. The British war debt next period expires on December 15, and the war debt issue is not one that can be agreed upon within five weeks. Therefore, the British government hopes that the same procedures previously passed in Lausanne will be implemented again, and that during the period of discussing this matter, or during the waiting period, the payment will be temporarily suspended. The British government believes that this matter should best begin in Washington, and as for other points, it will await the US government's expression of views. The French diplomatic note is roughly the same as the British diplomatic note, also requesting an extension of the Hoover suspension plan and reopening discussions on the entire war debt issue, saying that this move will have an extremely good impact on the global monetary panic. The French diplomatic note recalled the French government's automatic agreement to make major sacrifices in Lausanne and Stresa, and said that financial difficulties still hinder the restoration of international normal relations, and that new efforts must be made to break through these difficulties for the benefit of the whole. France's attitude at the two conferences in Lausanne and Stresa has proved that France sees the rapid economic recovery of Europe as being in its interest, and in this spirit, it is requesting a re-examination of the debt issue, and because the research cannot be completed in a short time, it is requested that the period of deferred payment be extended, so that the current major issue can be completed in an atmosphere of trust study.

▲ The National Society reported from London on the 13th that the British government sent a note to the United States last Thursday, consulting about discussing the entire structure of Anglo-American debt and requesting that payments on debts owed to the United States be temporarily suspended until the meeting is over. The full text of the long approximately seven hundred words, was published by the British Foreign Office today. The content involves asking the United States to convene a meeting with the United Kingdom to discuss debt issues in detail. However, it is not expected that the discussion will be completed before the payment date of December 15, so it is requested that the various payments due on that day be temporarily extended indefinitely. The memorandum solemnly states that world prosperity cannot be achieved until this matter is re-adjusted. Last year, President Hoover's proposal to suspend payments did not achieve the hope of realizing economic recovery. The Lausanne Agreement can be said to be the greatest contribution of the governments concerned to the early restoration of global prosperity in the international financial arena, but in order to achieve the goal, there must be cooperation from the United States. The proposal to suspend payment during the period of deliberation on this matter has been taken by the governments concerned to the United States today. As for the term limit, the memorandum has not mentioned the period in which the Anglo-American debt meeting is expected to end, and has only requested a temporary extension of payment during the meeting period or a period separately agreed upon, but it has expressed the hope that the United States will exchange views on this matter with the United Kingdom as soon as possible. It also claims that the scope of discussions at this type of meeting is so broad that an agreement cannot be reached in haste.

▲ The National Society reported from Washington on the 13th that the French memorandum to the United States was also released today, the content of which is briefer than that of the British memorandum, only asking the United States to continue to discuss the war debt issue and complete it in an atmosphere of mutual trust, following the precedent of the Lausanne Conference, before the resolution is reached, allowing a temporary suspension of payment. It also said that the French government's historical faith in this kind of step would help prevent the looming financial crisis in many countries. The proposals and the agreements reached in Lausanne have contributed to harmonizing international sentiment, economic recovery and the consolidation of peace. However, despite the Lausanne Agreement, the economic and financial difficulties that hinder the restoration of normalcy still exist. We must continue our efforts to eliminate them today to benefit the whole.

Hoover Expresses His Position

▲ Reuters reported from Washington on the 13th that President Hoover's attitude towards war debts has already been seen in his telegram to Roosevelt regarding the meeting at the White House next week to discuss war debts and other matters. Hoover still opposes any form of war debt cancellation, but the telegram stated that the United States could accept debtor nations not paying cash directly but giving equivalent compensation in other forms, such as opening up markets to accommodate US industrial and agricultural products. Furthermore, the substantial reduction of world armaments can reduce our burdens and dangers and is also related to the war debt issue. Hoover also said that if negotiations begin, there must be a long and detailed discussion that cannot be completed within his term of office (March 4). Negotiations will be restricted by Congress's rejection of war debt cancellation, and if Congress's attitude changes slightly, it will be changed by congressmen who follow Roosevelt as their leader. Therefore, although he is prepared to handle this issue within his power, for the welfare of the country, it must be handled with a common will. Therefore, he asked Roosevelt to call together key Democratic figures and others to jointly deliberate.

Borah Demands Disarmament

Senator Borah, chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, demanded that all countries actively reform their policies, saying that if such policies continue, they will destroy civilization, and the proposal to postpone payments should be accompanied by procedural guarantees that the situation will change thereafter. Republican Senator Bingham stated that he opposed the cancellation of war debts or the permission of repeated postponements of payment. However, at the same time, important figures, for the sake of American trade interests, advocated reorganizing the debts. They believe that completely canceling war debts is unnecessary economically and impossible in practice but advocate that Congress allow the re-consideration of the setting of debt repayment agreements and extend the existing suspension period to facilitate negotiations. The Baltimore Sun stated that there are currently only two options: debt offsetting or revision. Senators should not waste words on the cancellation of debts.

Congressional Attitude

▲ Reuters reported from Washington on the 13th that Senator Walsh, who is related to the highest Democratic Council, stated today that if the war debt issue is very urgent and needs to be dealt with immediately, then a special session of Congress should be convened immediately. Senator Swanson, who will replace Senator Borah as Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, stated that the American people do not want to take on the tax burden of foreigners and substitute themselves. Many indebted countries are superior to the United States in terms of industry and finance. Although responsible officials are unwilling to criticize the British and French notes, non-official circles believe that the United States cannot refuse to discuss with the two countries, but only Congress has the right to approve the extension of the debt period. Therefore, the postponement of the payment of debts due on December 15 may be a subject of debate in Congress. Congressional leaders claim that Democrats do not support the cancellation of war debts, but any reasonable proposal by Hoover and Roosevelt to postpone payments should receive a majority of support. However, if European politicians and European newspapers sing high praises in advance, recognizing that the atmosphere in the United States that allows an extension is a prelude to the cancellation of war debts in the future, it will hinder the matter.

▲ The National Society reported from New York on the 13th that the American International Debt Discussion Committee, a private organization, released a research report tonight, chaired by Sloan and endorsed by famous economists across the country, advocating that debtor nations be allowed to continue to postpone payments and that the entire debt issue be re-considered and adjusted. According to Sloan, this report has been directly requested by external economic experts for research, such as Smith, President of Columbia University, Bud, and Davis, who has the hope of becoming the future Secretary of State or Ambassador to the United Kingdom, all expressed their approval.

Roosevelt's Departure Date Undetermined

▲ The National Society reported from Albany on the 13th that Roosevelt remained at home today and did not go out to study the British and French war debt memorandums. It is said that Roosevelt has not fully recovered after catching a cold. He will probably be able to leave home for the office tomorrow. As for whether President Hoover's telegram inviting Roosevelt to Jinjing on Saturday has been received at this time, and which advisors Roosevelt is preparing to bring with him, the entourage refused to provide information. However, according to those close to Roosevelt, if Roosevelt accepts the invitation, Davis, Smith, and Buck are likely to be among those who will accompany him. However, whether Roosevelt will accept the invitation is still uncertain at this time. Some leaders believe that the President-elect will not have political power until March 4 of next year, and the Republican Party can resolve the matter on its own, advocating refusal to go. However, others say that Hoover has sincerely invited him in his personal capacity, which cannot be refused, because supporting the government is the duty of the people, so it is hoped that the Republican and Democratic parties can temporarily share the burden.

British Observations

▲ Reuters reported from London on the 13th that it was heard that all parties in the United Kingdom recognized this British diplomatic note as the first step in extremely important negotiations and acknowledged that the results of the US election would make it difficult for President Hoover to make a quick decision. The British are certain that the proposals contained in the British diplomatic note can be accepted by American public opinion. The British government believes that once the message that the United Kingdom and the United States have opened negotiations for the final settlement of British debt and that there will be no future payments is made public, the world's trust can be stabilized and the recovery of trade can be promoted. Reuters has learned that the British and French memoranda were drafted separately and are not identical. If negotiations are opened in the future, the British government will proceed with negotiations with other debtor nations on the one hand and follow the US's separate debt talks on the other hand, fearing that this memorandum will hinder the progress of the World Economic Conference. It is understood that the British owed US$95 million to the United States as of December 15. Furthermore, the total amount due is 460 million yuan, of which 20.2 million yuan of principal has been repaid, and 115 million yuan of interest is to be paid. As for the French debt to the United States, which is due at the same time, it is more than 19 million yuan. According to Reuters's New York dispatch, the British and French consultations with the United States on war debts have aroused blunt criticism from several parties.

▲ Havas reported from London on the 13th that this morning, the British press commented on the British government's request to extend the Hoover moratorium plan due to the war debt case. The Times stated that there was considerable reason to hope that the British proposal would be accepted by the United States, because if the financial contracts between countries were not revised, it would not be possible to seek recovery in the world economy. The Daily Telegraph reported that there was no other solution to the war debt issue except cancellation. The newspaper also said that Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain would personally go to Washington to preside over the negotiations in order to achieve the goal of cancellation. The Daily Telegraph also said that the Democratic Party will not implement its administration until four months later, and the decision on the war debt issue will therefore be delayed. As for the Chronicle, it believes that at present, neither the leaders of the Democratic Party nor the Republican Party are strongly opposed to revising the war debt repayment method. Therefore, it is feared that even if only an extension of the war debt due on December 15 is requested, it will be rejected by the US Senate and House of Representatives.

Japan will take advantage of this opportunity to take the most forceful stance, using withdrawal from the League of Nations to intimidate European and American countries. Japan will shift from delaying diplomacy to active offense. There are two reasons for this: one is due to the results of the US election and the war avoidance policies of the UK, US, and France; the other is that the situation in Japan is urgent, and the result of procrastination may lead to social revolution due to economic panic. It is better to cut it off and force a peace today with sufficient war preparations in order to eliminate the social unrest in Japan and the international instability of the puppet state.

Special Education News Feature: A More Scientific Teaching Guidance Plan (4) Du Gang

㈣ Formulation of the Plan

From analyzing the causes of deficiencies to discovering the need for guidance, instructors can formulate specific guidance plans based on this need to improve teaching. A teaching improvement guidance plan should include the following aspects: ㈠ Providing a better material environment to facilitate student work; ㈡ Providing better teaching tools; ㈢ Indicating better learning methods; ㈣ Indicating better teaching goals; ㈤ Providing better teaching materials; ㈥ Indicating better teaching methods. Therefore, a guidance plan does not only refer to "training teachers in service," but should also include various practical and research activities, such as creating tests, compiling teaching materials, and formulating teaching methods. The entire guidance plan should be consistent with the best educational implementation methods. That is, regarding the training of in-service teachers: ㈠ The objectives, content, and methods of the training plan should be based on scientifically established facts and principles; ㈡ Teachers should be provided with rich stimuli to enable them to recognize problems on their own; ㈢ The individual differences of teachers should be recognized, and different guidance techniques should be applied. A monotonous application of a certain guidance technique, such as distributing small publications on education, holding teacher conferences, or holding individual talks, should be avoided; ㈣ Instructors should provide sympathetic assistance for problems that humans cannot avoid and should not resort to dictatorial arbitrariness; ㈤ Instructors should encourage teachers' originality, self-control, and self-evaluation. Teaching guidance is a creative endeavor, and the personality of teachers should be considered everywhere, so that teachers do not lose self-confidence.

㈤ Measurement of Results

The effectiveness of teaching guidance should undoubtedly be measured. There are already many books published on the measurement of teaching effectiveness, but the measurement of teaching effectiveness guidance has hardly been mentioned in China. However, as the teaching guidance career gradually develops, objective measurement methods for guidance effectiveness will naturally develop with it. The scope of objective measurement of teaching guidance effectiveness is nothing more than the following aspects: ㈠ Measuring the effectiveness of guidance from the changes that occur in students, such as the number of students who are promoted, demoted, or drop out of school, as well as the effectiveness of learning in various aspects, etc.; ㈡ Measuring the effectiveness of guidance from the changes that occur in teachers, such as knowledge of subject matter, educational knowledge, psychological knowledge, teaching skills, and attitudes toward teaching, etc.; ㈢ Measuring the effectiveness of guidance from the changes that occur in teaching materials, teaching tools, and other teaching material conditions. In short, there is a need for objective and clear evidence of what positive effects teaching guidance has.

㈥ Application of Scientific Methods

Scientific methods must be used in both the implementation and research aspects of teaching guidance, such as: ㈠ The teaching guidance plan must be based on the results of scientific research on teaching; ㈡ The effectiveness of teaching guidance must be measurable. The basic principles of science are nothing more than measurement, changing several aspects of the environment under certain conditions, and then measuring the results; ㈢ Maintaining an experimental attitude. An instructor with an experimental attitude will never be satisfied with the status quo. In his attempts to improve teaching, new concepts, new plans, and new methods will naturally be generated. He will not stick to old ways but will instead plan to open up new paths. He will perseveringly study the effectiveness of various new improvement methods, pay attention to the reactions of teachers and students under various training plans, diagnose their deficiencies, analyze their causes, and then modify the plans and measure their effects again. He will continue to work hard in this way until the results are satisfactory.

What has been described in this article is only a general outline, and deficiencies in various aspects are inevitable. If there is an opportunity, the author will propose a detailed discussion on each aspect. Readers may wonder why the author has not proposed a specific plan in this article, but the author believes that a specific teaching guidance plan is formulated in response to a certain teaching situation. The instructor must go through investigation, diagnosis, and analysis before he can start to formulate it. In other words, before the instructor starts to formulate a plan, he must have a deep understanding of the current teaching situation and be able to effectively grasp where improvement and guidance are needed. Such a plan is specific, practical, and beneficial to teaching, but it also has limitations in time and space. Understanding this, the reader can know why the author does not propose a specific plan. As for the measurement of guidance efficiency, readers may think that the author is deliberately making shocking high-level arguments, but that is not the author's intention. In the process of teaching guidance, if there is no measurement step, then all the methods and techniques in the guidance process seem to have no destination. That is, the instructor may lose all control over his work and not know whether his work is effective or to what extent it is effective. If so, guidance cannot estimate its own work, let alone improve its own work. As for the tools for this kind of measurement, on the one hand, it can be aided by teaching tests, and on the other hand, it may be possible to engage in compilation. (End)

Salary-Demanding Representatives from Primary and Secondary Schools in Peiping to Go South Tonight

Peiping, 14th—Lang Xi-wu, Li Jing-han, Feng Liu-xi, Yao Shou-qi, and other salary-demanding representatives from primary and secondary schools, are scheduled to go south tomorrow night to urge the disbursement of 50,000 yuan in owed funds and to request the monthly allocation of funds, generally requesting the designation of tobacco and alcohol taxes or other tax revenues as a special fund for the Peiping municipal education fund. If the petition yields no results, the entire delegation will go south.

Educational Delegation from Europe and America Arrives in Paris

Paris, 13th—The Chinese and European-American faculty delegation that came to Europe to inspect various universities arrived here today from Berlin and was hosted by the Sorbonne University.

Wu County Primary School Principals' Conference

The Wu County Primary School Principals' Conference, held once in 1927, has been suspended for five years. Yesterday (14th), a meeting was held at the Dongzhai in the park. 158 principals attended, and 16 principals were absent. The meeting started at 9:00 AM. County Magistrate Zou presided over the meeting. Zhou Fo-hai, Director of the Education Department, accompanied by Secretary Chen Tian-ou, attended the meeting in Suzhou and gave instructions. Hu Huan-lian, Principal of Suzhou Middle School, and others also gave speeches. The ceremony was extremely grand. Shanghai Zhonghua Commercial Press, Datong and other bookstores sent personnel to present educational books. In the afternoon, discussions on proposals began, including 31 proposals on educational administration, 16 proposals on school administration, 8 proposals on research, and 15 proposals on economics. Due to the lack of time for lectures on the same day, the meeting may need to be extended by half a day until noon on the 15th before adjourning.

Changzhou County-Wide Boy Scout Inspection

The Boy Scouts of Wuyi County held a grand inspection and curriculum competition the day before yesterday. The Boy Scout General Association specially dispatched instructor Yang Ke-jing to Changzhou as the inspecting officer. In addition, the inspecting officers included Chen Bang-cai, secretary of the Provincial Council, Xue Di-gong, Sheng Jing-fu, Wang Chao-yi, Wang Zhang, and other members of the County Party Committee. The first place in the inspection was the County Middle School 646th Group, which scored 82 points. The first place in the competition was the County Middle School 646th Group for middle schools and the Bureau Front Street Primary School 152nd Group for primary schools, which were awarded prizes to encourage them.

Local Department Members Inspect Jiangnan College

Jiangnan College is currently submitting an application to the Ministry of Education for registration. The Ministry of Education dispatched three members, Guo Xin-song, Tong Guan-xian, and Shi Shang-kuan, to Shanghai to inspect the school. The members arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and went to the school on the 12th for detailed inspection. They will return to Nanjing on the 16th. It is also heard that the students of the school held a memorial week on the 14th and then held a welcome meeting for all the students. After the student representatives delivered a welcome speech, the three inspection members, Tong, Guo, and Shi, delivered speeches separately, elaborating on the importance of university education and the true meaning of studying social sciences, and also commended the current situation and future hopes of the school.

China Science Society Hosts Jiangsu Province Science Teachers

New Principal Appointed to Xitong Public School

Mr. Ross, the principal of the Han Bili Xitong Public School, has resigned. The Bureau of Works has now appointed Mr. Percy Crow as the new principal to take office from the spring of next year. Mr. Crow studied at Tom Bridge Middle School in his childhood and was the editor of the school magazine during his time at the school. In 1909, he entered Cambridge University and obtained a scholarship in ancient literature. He served as the captain of the debate team of his college during his time at the school and graduated with honors. He was then hired by the Ipswich College as a sixth-grade ancient literature teacher. The following year, when the European War broke out, he joined the artillery and became a lieutenant. He was promoted to battalion commander of the artillery. He was wounded four times and received two medals. After the armistice, he was assigned to be an instructor in the 161st Brigade. He retired in 1919 and returned to his teaching position. After 1920, he served as a teacher at Rochestede Middle School and coached the student army. Later, he went to Japan and became a teacher at the Naval Academy. In 1927, he joined the Bureau of Works, first at Nie Zhongcheng Public School and then at Han Bili Xitong Middle School, where he has been teaching until now.

Basketball New Technique (3)

(Original by Claire Byrchy) (Translated by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yi-qin)

In the game, if you can control the center jump, you will gain the upper hand and benefit a lot. This is generally recognized by coaches. This Chinese tactic was passed on to Hugh McDermott, coach of Oklahoma, who confirmed the effectiveness of this method at The Big Sin Conference. The center, No. 3, pats the ball to his right, then quickly turns to his left and runs down the sideline. First, No. 2 feigns a step forward to catch the center's patted ball, but in reality, No. 5 intercepts it and immediately passes or pats it to No. 1, who is crossing the court. No. 1 continues to dribble the ball forward in the predetermined direction. No. 2 tries to turn around his defender and head towards the basket. No. 1 then passes the ball to No. 2, who catches it and lifts it up forcefully and throws it to No. 3, so that it is put into the basket.

Free Talk

Two or One Branch

A Discussion of Tan Crab Anatomy by Zhan Lu

"September is for round navels, October is for sharp ones." Round for what? Round for divisions. Sharp for what? Sharp for the intensification of aggression.

Crabs are called messengers of the Jianghu (江湖, literally "rivers and lakes," referring to the martial arts world). These are crabs in the Jianghu, not crabs in the ocean. If they were sea crabs, they would never claim to be messengers of the Jianghu but would definitely call themselves overlords of the Pacific Ocean. They would roam wildly, leading their crab children and grandchildren to search for colonies, all armed to the teeth, calling it armed immigration. The thick shell is the crab's only protection; if not an armored car, it must be a tank.

The two pincers are used to clamp down on world opinion, so that even if you have the opportunity to speak, the place to speak is still silent and you cannot speak. If you want to speak, you must wait until it loosens its pincers.

Crabs are most afraid of redification. If they wear a bright red robe in the style of Hai Rui, the crab will not survive. Crabs are very averse to spicy things and perilla, unless they are caught and eaten by people. Then they are put in a pot and cooked with perilla. After they are cooked, they are dipped in mustard-flavored minced ginger and sent into the mouths of the old men. See how long you can run rampant? Only the remaining redified shells are thrown into

Can Military Force Be Relied Upon? 3

— You Xuan

After the First World War, the evil flames of militarism slightly subsided, and the trend of international peace gradually intensified. However, as time passed and the wounds began to heal, international jealousy arose, followed by an increasingly fierce arms race. There was a strong sense of returning to the era of militarism's rise from the late 19th century to the early 20th century. However, the evolution of history never repeats the same model. Nevertheless, the reaction of inertia often exists, and the current prevalence of militaristic aggression is clear proof. Japan's continental policy of plundering 3,767,700 square li of our Northeast Three Provinces' land and trampling upon our 30 million compatriots is truly an unprecedented act of violence in modern history. At this time, Japan could be said to be complacent, fulfilling its long-held desire to plot against us and achieving its ambition to annex the Asian continent. Although China is very weak and lacks strong resistance and fighting capabilities, with disaster imminent, it may not be willing to endure and await slaughter. Therefore, since the Mukden Incident and the fall of Jinzhou, although our authorities have been patient and cautious, patriotic people have disregarded life and death, rising up everywhere in the Northeast. Their weapons are inferior to the enemy's, but their national spirit is enough to inspire national development and awaken the sympathy of the world. The Japanese warlords, who are obsessed with military force, claim that their methods are brilliant and that they have mobilized the primitive aggressive spirit of their people, making the whole country united. In fact, it is a warlord monopoly to plan for "Manchuria," advance north to spy on Siberia, and advance south to erode North China. The military strength will be discussed later, but in terms of finance alone, they are already struggling to make ends meet and find it difficult to continue spending such huge military expenses. Those in Japan who are slightly aware of the situation feel that their situation is dangerous. Therefore, Finance Minister Takahashi, in examining the budget for the coming year, actually cut the military's new budget requests by half (the army's new request was cut by 164 million yuan (Japanese yen), and the navy's new request was cut by 287 million yuan). The military protested, with Army Minister Araki saying:

"...The general public believes that the army's new request for military equipment improvement funds is used to relieve small and medium-sized industrial and commercial businesses. This is a big mistake. The army, considering the overall national strength, national defense, and financial resources, believes that it is absolutely necessary, and never thought of relieving small and medium-sized businesses. If we give in on the budget案, then all these efforts will be in vain. Now is the critical moment, how can we give up halfway? So we must not be stingy with those 500 million or 1 billion yuan. For example, a young man asks for working capital. When working, he will naturally sweat, get tired, and even get slightly injured because of the work. However, he will recover quickly. Japan will definitely not perish..."

Considering Japan's current national strength, is it just sweating and fatigue? It is more than just being slightly injured. Businesses are trapped in the city, farmers are trapped in the countryside, and the total national treasury revenue is only 1,333 million Japanese yen, while expenditures exceed 2,230 million Japanese yen. Among them, the army and navy expenses (including increased budgets) are:

Army expenses: Total budget: 447,000,000 Japanese yen

Navy expenses: Total budget: 372,000,000 Japanese yen

Although these assumed figures have been repeatedly considered and carefully discussed by cabinet members, there are still fears that there will be various waves between the military and the cabinet, and between the cabinet and political parties. Saito is an ally of the navy, so no major problems may occur in the navy, but although the army temporarily expressed hesitation due to the increase of 50 million yuan, how can the warlords stop their aggressive ambitions and extravagant military spending? Since the budget for the coming year is unprecedentedly inflated, what will be the financial situation?

In recent years, Japan's national debt has increased dramatically. The visible financial situation for the coming year is as follows:

㈠ As of the end of September of this year, Japan's total national debt is 6.308 billion Japanese yen.

㈠ The amount of government bonds not yet issued this year is 614 million Japanese yen.

㈠ The amount of government bonds delivered is 61 million Japanese yen.

㈠ The amount of temporary loans is 658 million Japanese yen.

㈠ The amount of government bonds to be issued in the coming year is at least 1 billion Japanese yen.

㈠ According to the current market price of the Japanese yen, the increase in foreign debt due to the low exchange rate is approximately 1.5 billion Japanese yen.

The total of the above six items should be over 10.1 billion. Previously, the author speculated that Japan's national debt would increase to 10 billion in two or three years, reaching one-tenth of Japan's total national wealth. If such debt increases so sharply, how can the exhausted people of Japan bear it? However, the Japanese cabinet believes that "1 billion or 5 billion should not be spared." The national struggle between China and Japan cannot be resolved in three or five years. If the Chinese people can continue to persist in this long-term, disguised war, Japan's military spending in the Northeast will inevitably increase with the years. After five, ten, or fifty years, Japan's existing national wealth will be completely scattered in smoke and bullets, and consumed on guns and knives. We recall that during the reign of Louis XIV of France, France was not strong, but its only fatal wound was its financial breakdown. Compared to the relative aspect of its national strength, the Japan of today may not exceed France at that time, and the consumption of military expenses is far greater than that of France at that time. It is also the first among the countries in the world, intending to break world peace and deliberately challenge, which is also the Germany before the war. Public justice cannot control its power, what will the iron-blooded lessons be?

Securities and Salt Tax Rebound Strongly by One Yuan 31

| Other types rose from six or seven jiao to one yuan |

| Transactions totaled over 5.7 million |

Yesterday, the situation at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was generally not dull. The sentiment of buyers and sellers was moderate, but because there was greater market demand, sporadic investments from various parties bought in, with buying being more active than selling. As a result, all prices rebounded compared to the end of last week. However, because the sentiment of buyers was dispersed, the market seemed to favor forward transactions, with no large transactions from major players. Therefore, although prices trended upward, the momentum was quite moderate. The prices rose immediately upon opening in the morning, and then fluctuated and gradually strengthened without any major changes. As a result, compared to the previous day, the salt tax rose by 1.2 yuan, the troop reduction tax rose by over 1 yuan, and the 1929 loan also rose by about seven or eight jiao. Observing the situation in the bond market, the market sentiment remained good, and there may be a possibility of further price increases. However, based on the current environment, it seems unlikely that there will be any major changes in the short term. New York Stock Market Slightly Up 32

Xin Feng Foreign Firm reports that the New York Stock Exchange market situation last Saturday (the 12th) did not fluctuate much. From October 22nd to 29th, the number of freight cars totaled 588,000, a decrease of 29,259 from the previous week. On the day after the election, stocks fell sharply, but the market's absorption power was great, so it was generally considered a constructive technical indication. As for trading, there was a significant improvement compared to before, but most investors still did not participate. Overall, the current stock market situation may continue to advance, but prudent investors should wait and see, waiting for the stock market's strength to be fully demonstrated. Cotton Market Arrives Sparsely, Showing Hardening 36

| Difficult for General Yarn Factories |

The cotton market is gradually showing signs of hardening because prices in various producing areas are difficult to fall, and sources from all directions remain sluggish. Although the upward force of American cotton is weak, there is also a lack of downward trends. Most sellers, seeing this situation, have some hedges, and fewer new sellers are emerging, so the market tends to be tight. However, yarn sales are too dull, and factory demand is still quiet, although foreign factories occasionally purchase. Because the arrival of cotton has decreased, the trend of the cotton market is higher than that of the yarn market, making it even more difficult for yarn factories.

Active Arrival and Sales of Ke Xian Rice 41

| Looking Up to the Future Market |

Yesterday, there was no market for foreign rice. Over 3,000 bags of Ke Xian rice newly arrived. Fujianese merchants still had a keen interest, and merchants from Tianjin also began to inquire, so the market was able to hold up. There was a stronger interest in commercial Ke Xian rice, while the interest in medium-grade rice was slightly weaker. Therefore, commercial goods have rebounded by two jiao compared to the lowest market price last week, while medium-grade rice remains flat. The unified market opened with 1,200 bags of Hunan Ji Jing rice priced at 8 yuan, 7 jiao, 5 fen to 6 jiao, and 310 bags of Ji You rice priced at 9 yuan, 1 jiao to 9 yuan. There were 300 bags of Ji Yuan rice priced at 10 yuan and 5 fen to 10 yuan. There were 300 bags of Jiangxi Ji Wan priced at 8 yuan, 6 jiao, 5 fen to 6 jiao. Jiangxi Ji Wan was purchased by merchants from Tianjin, while Hunan rice was purchased by merchants from Fujian. There are 3,500 bags of Xiang rice in the market, and there are also 2,000 to 3,000 bags of goods in transit. Jiangxi rice arrives and is sold immediately, with no accumulation. Only a small number of goods in transit are being shipped. However, the interest of merchants from the north and south revived yesterday and today. In addition to the opening of the market, there are also traders who personally match customers, so the future market may be stable.

Changshu Rice Prices Plummet 42

| Highest Grade Opens at Six Yuan Five Jiao |

The most important commercial center in Changshu is the rice industry. The rice industry relies entirely on rural farmers. Since the bumper harvest this autumn, rice prices have been falling day by day. Although the government has repeatedly tried to provide relief, it has been in vain. Therefore, in recent days, ordinary farmers have been forced to pay rent and taxes, and have no ability to store rice. They have to transport all the rice to the market for sale. Due to the instability of bank turnover, market prices have suddenly fallen. In the past three days, the decline has reached more than one yuan. The highest grade of goods is no more than six yuan and five jiao, the middle grade is six yuan, and the low grade has fallen to below five yuan. It is learned from people in the rice industry that, given the tight money supply and the influence of the Shanghai rice market, the rice market will likely plummet. In terms of prices, it will be difficult to improve, and prices will continue to fall. Rice traders are all frowning and suffering heavy losses.

Flour Market Gradually Entering Good Territory 43

| | The Power of Major Players Holding Up the Market | |

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the prices of foreign wheat rose by about three, four, five, or six jiao, so the sentiment for each month was active. Buying sentiment was temporarily strong, and empty positions were quickly covered. Moreover, the attitude of manufacturers was ambiguous. Although the general view was that with rice prices being very loose and unusually loose for years, flour seemed to have no reason to be exclusively strong. However, the standard situation was slightly different, and once it was held up, it felt powerful. Entering a good phase was probably due to this. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, it seemed soft for a while because local small factories and factories along the Yangtze River still had listings, and people's sentiment seemed tired. However, due to the major players holding up the market and not wanting to let go, it remained stable. It is difficult to predict the market prospects because the market is no longer regular. Because urgent shipments of Australian wheat are still only three taels and five qian, this situation is not good for the future. As a result, this month rose by one fen compared to the previous weekend, December rose by 7.5 li, January-February rose by one fen, and March rose by one fen and 2.5 li. April rose by one fen and a half.

Wheat Futures Stable Only 44

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally stable for all months. The prices of foreign wheat rose by about three, four, five, or six jiao, so people's sentiment was naturally stable. However, there was very little difference in the reported increase in foreign wheat futures in reality. Because there are few chips for the current standard's firmness, if it rises again, Australian wheat may tend to trap people. The current pricing is already considered possible, and the market's atmosphere is not showing excitement because of this. As a result, this month rose by one fen, March rose by one fen, and April rose by two fen. Spot wheat transactions were slightly more active, with Gaoyou wheat opening at 3 taels and 3.5 qian and Luhe wheat at 3 taels, 3 qian, and 4 fen, totaling over 800 bags.

[P Dried Longan Is Predicted to Fall After Prolonged Stagnation]

In addition, inferior goods from Hankou, Tianjin, and other places have been transported at very low prices, which has had a significant impact. More than 800 boxes were transacted in the city. The top price for Zhenmei was 55 taels, and the top price for Xioumei was 33 taels, with no rise or fall compared to before. For the first-class Zhenmei, traders only had a few negotiations, and the market was sluggish. For Gongxi green tea, the Russian Aid Association and white-collar traders are both taking a wait-and-see attitude, and the market is also very deserted.

The British plate was more stable at 7.5 cents and sold for 5 taels and 9 qian and a half. Only No. 16 and No. 18 of new lead wire were slightly traded yesterday, and few other colors were touched. In addition, bamboo joints, water cement, angle iron, and mouth iron were all traded, but there were no ups and downs in the market.
