Qiu Changsheng and Others Sued by Paternal Uncle for Encroaching on Store Property 140

Qiu Changsheng, son of the deceased wealthy paint merchant Qiu Weiqing, and his nephew Qiu Qiyuan, were sued in the First Special District Court by their paternal uncle Qiu Hengcai, represented by lawyer Jiang Yiping, for encroaching on store property. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened the court to summon them for questioning. The two defendants hired lawyers Wu Linkun, Li Zuyu, Tao Jiachun, and Qin Liankui to defend them. According to the plaintiff, the charges against the defendants for encroachment were divided into two parts: 1) Regarding the Dechangrun Paint Store, the store was established by Qiu Weiqing in the 20th year of the Guangxu reign by selling seven mu of ancestral farmland, which was valued at 350 yuan, as capital. Therefore, there were annual dividends. From the 15th year of the Republic of China to the 20th year, I only did not take money from the store for 16 years. Otherwise, I would take 300 or 500 yuan at the end of each year to spend the New Year at home. Now this right has been deprived by the defendants. 2) Regarding the Yitian (charitable farmland), Qiu Weiqing, because of the profits of Dechangrun, withdrew funds from the surplus and purchased 3,000 mu of Yitian in the Ben Niu area, which he donated to the clan. Now this Yitian has also been stolen and sold. But this matter is recorded in Qiu Weiqing's obituary, which the defendants cannot deny. In response, Qiu Changsheng stated that Dechangrun was established by his late father in partnership with Qiyuan's grandfather Hengde and Zhao Yulin, with a capital of 3,000 taels of silver. The plaintiff had no shared rights. As for the Yitian, he had only heard his late father say that he had purchased 120 mu and donated it to the clan's ancestral hall. Lawyers Wu and Tao then presented various written evidences to prove that the plaintiff had absolutely no relationship with Dechangrun, saying that the plaintiff had fabricated facts and brought a false accusation, requesting that the case be dismissed. The plaintiff's lawyer, Jiang Yiping, requested that the account books of Dechangrun over the years be subpoenaed for investigation, which would make the source of its capital clear. As for the existence of the Yitian, he requested that Qiu Weiqing's obituary be consulted. Judge Huang then ordered that the case be adjourned to the afternoon of the 24th of this month for continued hearing, and ordered the defendants to bring the account books to the court at that time for verification.

Owes Too Much Money; Falsely Reports Robbery

Zhu Ronggui Daydreams 141

Zhu Ronggui, 43 years old, from Huzhou, who lives at No. 33 Dongde'an Lane, Shanxi Road, in the Public Concession and runs a Huzhou crepe business, went to the Daxizhao police station in the French Concession at around 7 PM the night before last to report that he was robbed by four bandits who blocked his path while he was walking on the Huangpu beach in Xinkai River. He claimed that 330 silver dollars were stolen, and requested an investigation. The detective Zhou Ruzhang was immediately dispatched to investigate and found that there was no robbery. Zhu had falsely reported the robbery. He reported the situation to the head detective, who took Zhu into custody. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Yuan Jiahong stated the facts of the case, and said that the police were prosecuting Zhu for falsely accusing public officials without specifying the offender, in accordance with Article 182 of the Criminal Law, and requested a trial. The detective Zhou Ruzhang also reported that last night, the head detective ordered him to take the defendant to the scene of the incident to investigate the robbery. On the way, the defendant said to him, "Please help me. I owe too much money, so I had to falsely report the robbery." Therefore, he took him into the police station for detention. When questioned, Zhu Ronggui admitted that he had indeed falsely reported the robbery because he was in debt and wanted to delay his creditors. He was evasive about other matters. Judge Wu verified the confession and ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody pending sentencing.

Tuberculosis Sanatorium Medical Report 142

The medical report of the Shanghai Tuberculosis Sanatorium on Daxi Road No. 2 for the last quarter is as follows: 205 initial diagnoses, 657 follow-up visits, 147 X-ray examinations, and a total of 101 hospitalizations. The majority of the patients were discharged in good condition, with a mortality rate of 7%. A total of 305 patients were referred for consultation. Among the patients with third-stage cavitary tuberculosis, artificial pneumothorax was performed in 32% of the cases. The results were mostly transformed from danger to safety, with excellent results. Currently, there are two patients who have been hospitalized for surgery for more than three months, and their weight has increased by as much as 15 pounds. The hospital hopes that hospitals and sanatoriums will uniformly adopt this equipment to achieve rapid results.

Recent News from Zhanghua Woolen Mill in Pudong

Discarded Steam Engines; Purchased Large Amount of Electricity 143

The Zhanghua Woolen Textile Mill in Zhoujiadu, Pudong, has a strong capital and a large scale. It weaves various woolen fabrics with excellent quality and very low prices. The Chinese people are vying to buy them, recovering many rights and interests. Recently, the new manager Cheng Nianpeng and the factory director Tong Luqing have carefully planned and worked for improvement. The factory's power originally came from a 240-horsepower steam engine. However, because it consumed too much coal, it was not economical and the amount of energy limited expansion. Now, it has reached an agreement with the Pudong Electric Company to have electricity supplied by the company. It is reported that the price of electricity is very low, which can save a lot of expenses every month. Moreover, the company has ample power and can be expanded at any time, which is very convenient. In the future, the factory's products will be more exquisite because the motor speed is uniform, and the price will be gradually reduced because the cost is lower. This is good news for the domestic goods industry.

Vietnamese Policeman Oversteps Boundary and Beats a Vegetable Vendor

Vegetable Stalls Arouse Public Outrage 144

Wu Tongwei, 38 years old from Yancheng, makes a living by selling vegetables. He lives at No. 3, Defu Lane, Tangjiawan. Yesterday morning, Wu carried two baskets of vegetables to sell at the junction of the Chinese and French Concessions in Tangjiawan. At around 11 AM, a Vietnamese policeman (name translated as Da Qie, 25 years old) from No. 32, Songshan Road Police Station in the French Concession, passed by on patrol with a gun and drove Wu away. Wu argued that the place was in the Chinese Concession and that the policeman should not interfere. The Vietnamese policeman became enraged, put his gun in a shop, and took an iron pliers to beat Wu. Wu's head was severely injured and bleeding profusely. At the same time, all the vegetable stalls were outraged. Fortunately, police officer Zhang Shaowu from post No. 17, who was standing there, heard the noise and arrived. He took Wu and the Vietnamese policeman, along with the iron pliers, to the Second District Headquarters. After questioning by District Chief Jin, the Vietnamese policeman said that Wu had bitten his finger. Soon after, the Songshan Road Police Station heard the news and sent translator Fei Xiangxian and detective Xitan to the Second District. Initially, they requested that Wu Tongwei and the Vietnamese policeman be transferred to the police station. District Chief Jin sternly refused and agreed only to take the Vietnamese policeman away. The detective then issued a receipt and took the policeman away to have his injuries examined at the hospital. Wu Tongwei was also filed with the local court for a medical examination.

Fake Detective Turns on a Real Detective

Tong Yuchun's Intimidation of Removing a Brokerage House Causes an Uproar 145

Lin Yiqin, from Ningbo, is in the hardware business. In August of this year, he obtained goods worth 65 taels of silver from Shi Ruimo of Yisheng Hardware Store at No. 994 Broadway Road. He paid with a check from Tongyuan Qianzhuang. When Shi went to collect the money, he negotiated with Lin, and Lin changed the check to a guarantee, agreeing to pay the money on the 10th of this month. However, he did not fulfill the agreement. On the 12th, at 5:30 PM, they negotiated at Tong Yuchun Teahouse at No. 508 Fujian Road. Shi arrived on time, but Lin invited more than ten people, including Wang Baodi from Nanjing, to intimidate Shi and force him to return Lin's guarantee. A dispute arose and Shi shouted for help. At this time, Chinese detectives Zheng Huaili and Chen Dabao from the Huishi Police Station were ordered to take Yao Sandu, the victim of a theft case at No. 148 North Shanxi Road, to identify and arrest the bandits. They passed by and heard the noise and went forward to inquire. Wang Baodi suddenly claimed to be a Chinese detective from the Laozha Police Station, prohibiting Zheng and others from interfering, and arrested Zheng and Chen, insisting on taking them to the police station. The two detectives refused to obey and were all taken to the Laozha Police Station. After investigation by detective Cao Qishan, it was found that Wang was not a detective from the police station, but an imposter. Wang Baodi and Lin Yiqin were arrested and sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Judge Qian Hongye sat in court to interrogate Wang and Lin. Lawyers Fan Gang and Tang Huaiqun defended them. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated the facts of the case and said that he was prosecuting them for attempted intimidation under Article 370, Paragraph 3 of the Criminal Law, and for obstructing the duties of public officials under Article 165 of the same law, requesting severe punishment. Zheng Huaili, Chen Dabao, Shi Ruimo, and Yao Sandu then filed cases, proving the behavior of the defendants. When questioned, the two defendants denied the allegations. Lin said that Shi had previously owed him 200 yuan and gave him a bad check for 60 yuan. This time, he owed Shi 65 taels, and after paying 22 taels, he still owed 43 taels. Therefore, he invited Shi to Tong Yuchun the day before yesterday to discuss a solution. He did not expect Shi to be ashamed and angry and collude with the detectives to falsely accuse him of intimidation. Judge Qian said that it was necessary to investigate the Tong Yuchun Teahouse in this case and adjourned the hearing. Lawyer Tang requested that the two defendants be released on bail, which Qian approved. Wang and Lin each posted 2,000 yuan bail and were released pending trial.

Ma Shungen, 19 years old, son of Ma Shousheng from Pudong, originally learned to be a tailor in his hometown, but dropped out midway. Special Cases

Report on the Situation of the Shanghai Public Concession by Judge Fei Tang, Volume 4 (23) 177

Summary of the Proposed Regulations

1. Employees listed in the permanent staff register, hereinafter referred to as "permanent employees," should be allowed to maintain their positions if their conduct is excellent, they are loyal to their duties, and they are indeed competent, until they have completed twenty years of service and reached the age of fifty, and thus become eligible to receive what is now called the "minimum pension." However, if there is any reason listed in the regulations, the Municipal Council may dismiss any employee before completing twenty years of service, in accordance with the remuneration stipulated in the regulations, or a portion of the pension calculated in proportion to the years of service, or other.

2. Establish a Municipal Government Service Committee (hereinafter referred to as the Committee) to handle issues arising between the Municipal Council and any permanent employee.

3. Any permanent employee who is accused of misconduct (the meaning of this term includes disobedience, offending superiors, and dereliction of duty) must first be investigated by the Committee before being dismissed, demoted, or have their salary deducted. However, this does not apply if the employee concerned abandons his right to request an investigation. After investigation, if the Committee believes that the employee is indeed guilty of misconduct and that the circumstances are serious enough to warrant dismissal, demotion, or salary deduction, the Municipal Council may dismiss, demote, or deduct the salary of the employee for misconduct; otherwise, it may not do so.

4. Any permanent employee who voluntarily resigns before becoming eligible to receive the minimum pension (i.e., completing twenty years of service and reaching the age of fifty) in accordance with the current rules, and whose resignation is deemed by the Committee to be due to some actual or proposed major change in his position or conditions of service, and that it would be unfair in the circumstances to force the employee to accept this position or conditions without allowing him to receive a portion of the pension calculated in proportion to his years of service, shall be entitled to receive a portion of the pension calculated in proportion to his years of service.

5. In addition to misconduct, the following circumstances may be considered legitimate reasons for the Municipal Council to dismiss an employee before he becomes eligible to receive the minimum pension:

A. Continued illness not due to the employee's own fault (Note 1).

B. Inability to perform duties due to an accident beyond the employee's control and not as a result of public service.

C. Abolishing the position, or reducing, reorganizing, or streamlining various parts or offices of municipal administration, or improving the part or office to which the employee belongs to save expenses or increase efficiency.

6. If any committee of the Municipal Council recommends that the Council exercise its power to dismiss a permanent employee for any of the reasons mentioned above (Articles 5A, 5B, and 5C), the employee may request that the recommendation be submitted to the Municipal Government Service Committee for consideration before being submitted to the Board of Directors for a vote, and may submit a written opinion to the Committee. The Committee shall consider the matter in a timely manner and investigate it in the manner it deems appropriate. If oral evidence is accepted, the employee shall be given the opportunity to make a personal appeal, and the results of the investigation and consideration shall be reported to the Board of Directors. After considering the report, the Board of Directors shall be free to decide whether to accept the recommendation of the Municipal Council Committee.

7. The proposed Municipal Government Service Committee may be organized in the following manner:

The committee members should be elected annually, with at least five and at most seven members, and should include the following:

Two or more members elected by the Board of Directors, but the elected members need not be limited to directors.

One or more senior officials recommended by the heads of various departments of the Municipal Council (to be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Hút Tiao (Nonsense) 178

— Fó (Buddha)

| Ten Ways to Get Along in the World |

Whether it's Xipi, Erhuang, Eighteen Touches, Four Seasons Longing, Nine Tunes Eighteen Variations, if every tune harmonizes, that's Hút Tiao. The term Hút Tiao wasn't originally used this way, so I use Hút Tiao instead of harmonious tune, but that's pretty much the common usage nowadays.

The term Hút Tiao has been around for a long time. During the reign of Emperor Min of Jin, Shi Le arrested Wang Jun. Jun scolded, "You Hút slave, how dare you tease me, you are so ferocious and rebellious!" That was the beginning of Hút Tiao. The Hút Tiao used today is mostly harmonious but not Hút Tiao. If the Hút Tiao is not done right, you add a blind person, calling it "blind Hút Tiao," or add the word "làn" (bad), calling it "làn Hút Tiao." Mixing everything together, that's Hút Tiao; being able to get around every situation, that's Hút Tiao; doing whatever your friends ask you to do, that's also Hút Tiao. Hút Tiao is truly a wonderful art of getting along in the world.

When Party A is in power, I express my goodwill towards Party A, that's Hút Tiao; when Party B loses power, I express my disappointment towards Party B, that's also Hút Tiao; when Party A says something is good, I say it's truly outstanding; when Party B says something is bad, I say it's truly useless, truly a mistake. Emperor Taizong of Tang once stopped under a tree and said, "This is a good tree." Yuwen Shiji followed suit, praising it without end. The emperor said sternly, "Wei Zheng once admonished me to stay away from sycophants. I didn't know who the sycophant was, I suspected it was you but wasn't sure. Today, it's confirmed." This is Hút Tiao that was seen through. During the reign of Han Tuozhou in the Song dynasty, Zhao Shiduo echoed him. Tuozhou once toured the Southern Garden with guests, passed a mountain village, looked at the bamboo fence and thatched cottage, and said, "This is truly the atmosphere of the countryside, but it lacks the crowing of chickens and barking of dogs." Suddenly, they heard a dog barking from the thicket, and saw that it was Shiduo. Tuozhou laughed loudly. This is Hút Tiao that was not seen through.

Yuwen Shiji and Zhao Shiduo were both masters of Hút Tiao. Shiji was unfortunate to encounter Emperor Taizong of Tang, and thus failed. Zhao Shiduo was fortunate to encounter Han Tuozhou, so his Hút Tiao succeeded. So Hút Tiao can be fortunate or unfortunate?

Màn Great Sale, True Great Sale, Resist Japanese Goods, Swear to Resist Japan, Share National Crisis, Long-term Resistance Signboard, Lù Gǎo Jiàn (a famous ham brand), True Lù Zhì

Is it the time to serve the country with literature?

A man with ambition should also be like this.

The Han family expanded its territory by thousands of miles every day,

Not counting the lyrics bought at Changmen.

I also know that the border affairs are too chaotic,

Which is stronger, a Mauser or a writing brush?

Shame on the scholars who talk about saving the country,

Idly composing ten thousand-word chapters.

Science

Translation of Scientific Common Sense 180

— (Excerpted from the Commentary Weekly)

Most of the lead powder or limestone comes from the remains of living things.

When jumping from a balloon with a parachute, if the parachute is not opened, the rate can reach 120 miles per hour.

Not only are animals and plants subject to the ravages of microorganisms, but so are rocks. Today's farmland and mountain forest soils are the result of microbial erosion of rocks.

Metschnikoff said that ancient people hoped to die early when they were old, considering it a natural result, just like hoping to sleep every evening.

The global ocean volume is more than 319 million cubic miles, and the Pacific Ocean volume is 167 million cubic miles, accounting for more than half.

Artificial silk is made from the head of Indian bamboo according to experiments.

Hale said that if an airplane pilot breathes oxygen for one hour before ascending, completely exhaling the light gas in the body, he can fly to a height of ten miles without any danger.

The deepest part of the global ocean is in the Mindanao Deep near the Philippine Islands, which is 35,400 feet deep. The Alqie Deep north of New Zealand is 30,930 feet deep.

The heaviest substance in the world is (Osmiyrn), the lightest substance is hydrogen, the softest is gold, and the most valuable is , which sells for $2 million per ounce.

The pathogens of yellow fever, spotted fever, smallpox, plague, trachoma, rabies, measles, and other diseases cannot be seen even with a high-powered microscope, and can be filtered through microbial filters.

The skin has four kinds of sensations, namely warm, cold, pain, and touch, each connected to various tissues of the body. Some parts only feel warm, some parts only feel cold, and there is no effect elsewhere.

Body size is related to climate regulation. Animals with large bodies lose heat more slowly, so animals with smaller bodies must breathe more objects to make up for the lost heat.

If the Earth encounters a major earthquake and expands by 200 meters (650 feet), Japan and the Malay Archipelago will be connected to Asia. The three British Isles will be connected to Europe, and all of America will be connected to Asia. Conversely, if the Earth shrinks by 200 meters, Japan will disappear without a trace, and European countries will become small tribes. The United States will lose its eastern and southern states, and Brazil and Argentina will also disappear without a trace. China will remain unchanged except for the deltas of the Yellow River and the Yangtze River.

School Scene

University Professor 181

— Jiā Lǐ

"Clang... Clang..."

The bell for class at a certain university in western Shanghai was ringing crisply. In the midst of this continuous bell ringing, the students taking Applied Chinese Composition filed into Classroom 63.

Mr. Zhang, the professor teaching this course, was an old man over half a century old. He was very tall and spoke in a very loud voice, but sometimes it was mixed with a "lā kuài" (patter) accent. Today, as usual, he carried his three-foot-long "stick," raised his head wearing a melon-skin cap, and straightened his chest as he slowly walked into Classroom 63.

The noisy voices in the classroom immediately subsided, and the students, one by one, held their breath and looked at the words written by the teacher on the blackboard, listening to the teacher criticizing the articles in the book.

Page 19

On the blackboard was written "Official Document Format, page 42, example 30." What the teacher was criticizing was, of course, this article.

The teacher read aloud, "The Judicial Investigation Committee's submission to the National Government, excerpt, requesting the promulgation of the Civil Code"... "Now that the Civil Code has not been promulgated, the judicial basis is the existing laws of the former Qing Dynasty, which are incomplete and inadequate. If the laws are exhausted, then the judges will use what they call 'principles' to make arbitrary judgments, which is extremely dangerous to determining the rights of the people." He paused and said, "The most important thing in reading articles is to understand their meaning. You see, this passage clearly says that the existing laws are not good, right?"

He then continued to read aloud, "The draft Civil Code compiled by the Law Compilation Bureau of the former Qing Dynasty selected the most essential legal principles of the civil codes of various countries, and sent personnel to investigate the customs of various provinces. It was carefully and thoroughly compiled to become this law." The teacher finished reading this section with great excitement and began to criticize it, saying:

"The Civil Code protects civil rights. The political systems of the former Qing Dynasty and the Republic of China are different, so the laws of the former Qing Dynasty cannot be applied to the Republic of China. You see, doesn't the opening of this submission say that the existing laws are not good? But then it's wrong, saying that the draft Civil Code selected the most essential legal principles of the civil codes of various countries, what investigation of customs, careful and thorough compilation, and so on to become this law. The existing laws are the draft Civil Code. Opposing it in the first place and then agreeing with it later, the former words don't match the latter, isn't that a big loophole?" He said all of this in one breath, paused, and moved his smiling face, like an automatic fan used in the summer, from the south side of the classroom all the way to the north side. Looking at the students, one by one sat in silence, some nodding frequently, as if to say, "The teacher's criticism is really good." Some opened their mouths and laughed, as if to say, "The teacher's criticism has made us suddenly enlightened!"

"..."

"Teacher!" A student suddenly broke the silence, awakening the teacher's fantasy, and said, "Teacher, you're mistaken! The existing laws and the draft Civil Code are not the same thing. The existing laws are the existing laws, and the draft Civil Code is the draft Civil Code!"

"Ha! Ha! Ha!" The classroom was suddenly filled with laughter, because everyone couldn't hold it in any longer.

The teacher was embarrassed by this. He quickly defended himself, saying, "Even if they are two different things, what I'm criticizing is the style of writing! From the point of view of the style of writing, this article is not good after all! If you don't believe me, I'll revise it for you to see. I just need to change two words, and the style of writing will be smooth."

The student said, "I'm saying that the teacher has confused the facts. I didn't say that the teacher's article is not good. The teacher's article is certainly brilliant!"

The laughter was about to start, but they had to hold it back again, because another student spoke. He said, "Teacher, let's not worry about the facts now, it doesn't matter. Teacher, please continue to talk about the style of writing!"

"Ha! Ha! Ha!" Everyone laughed even harder!

"Clang... Clang..." The bell rang outside, saving the teacher's life.

The students stood up like a tide, squeezing out of the classroom with smiles on their faces.

What about the teacher? With his head lowered, his waist bent, his "stick" dragging, like a dog that has lost its home, he hurried away to the teachers' lounge! (Moved to help the Northeast Volunteers)

Rape Case

Revenge 182

— Wu

Ever since Huang Tianfu discovered his wife had a lover, he decided to find a way to retaliate. How could a dignified man be a cuckold? Moreover, all the neighbors knew. Humph! This was simply a lifelong humiliation. So he thought:

"Yes, I must retaliate, I absolutely must retaliate. But how to retaliate? What method to use? The only way is to kill her, and kill the adulterer too. One day, when I know they are trysting, I can use the best pistol to shoot them both, one bullet through two people's chests! Ah! That bright red blood, how satisfying that would be! Of course, a man should have such ambition... But where does the best pistol come from? Buy it? Where would I get so much money? Borrow it? There's no way... Right, I can buy a knife, a sharp blade, that would be the same, and personally drawing blood would be even more satisfying! ... No, that won't do, that adulterer is a burly man, and he worships that old rogue, every rogue is skilled in martial arts, I'm not sure I can beat him. Right, this is not good, too risky, not worth risking my life for a woman. So what to do? Undoubtedly, I must retaliate. Oh, right, I can just kill my wife alone, that's no problem, surely a man can beat a woman? No, kill the woman and leave the adulterer? That would be too spineless. Besides, "to catch adulterers, catch both," killing only the woman, without evidence, wouldn't I be the one going to jail? How could that work?... But I have to retaliate! Hmm, right, I can commit suicide, without killing either the adulterer or the adulteress. After I die, others will surely know why I died, of course, someone will definitely scold her, curse her, let her be criticized by society, let her bear the stigma of infidelity until death. This way she will be ashamed and have nowhere to hide, she will never be able to face anyone. Oh! That would be more satisfying than killing her. Yes, I must commit suicide! Suicide! ... But suicide is dying myself, how terrible that is! I still have many good days to live, and many beautiful things are waiting for me, why should I commit suicide? That's such a stupid thing to do! But... yes, I can leave her, immediately tell her to leave me, sever our relationship as husband and wife, isn't that also a method of retaliation? Of course, if I abandon her, I won't be a cuckold, this way, no one will be killed, no one has to die, isn't that a perfect solution? Right, I must do this."

That's what Huang Tianfu finally decided. Not long after, his beloved wife, with whom he had shared a bed for many years, went to live with her lover under his own wife-selling contract. However, his children were deeply resentful and wept bitterly from then on, even though he often comforted himself with generosity.

Short Story

Superstitious Poison 183

— Yixin

Inside a high wall, there is a new house, looking grand and beautiful from the gate. The furnishings in the hall are all dazzling, indicating that this is a wealthy family. An old woman is in the courtyard, threading a string of plain beads while murmuring "Namo Amitabha." Namo Amitabha. At this moment, two young men in Western suits walk in from outside, holding briefcases, and approach the old woman. One of the young men, holding the briefcase, says: "Old woman, we are here on behalf of the Northeast Volunteer Army to raise donations. In this cold weather, the Northeast is even colder, already a world of ice and snow. The poor Volunteer Army, in this world of ice and snow, is still working hard to kill the enemy. With such courage, we are here to raise money to prepare silk-padded coats so they won't be cold and can kill more dwarfs. Please help with a few hundred dollars."

(The old woman, upon hearing the young man's request for several hundred dollars, immediately glares at him and says: Humph! You have quite an appetite, does my family have that much money to help them? No, no, please go to someone else's house. Namo Amitabha, Namo Amitabha.

(Young man) If you don't have much, twenty dollars, ten dollars, is also fine, it doesn't matter. First, it's the old woman's patriotic zeal. Second, it's also charity, to prevent them from freezing to death, a great good deed.

(Old woman) Humph! I don't want to give a penny. They are constantly fighting, each seeking their own livelihood. Now they are fighting with the Japanese. Bodhisattva, may you manifest and make them all freeze to death, so there will be

peace and quiet, how wonderful would that be? Namo Amitabha, Namo Amitabha.

Another young man says: We misjudged, this tall building is actually the home of a slave to a fallen nation.

The old woman snorts! "Slave to a fallen nation or not, it has nothing to do with you. We have the Bodhisattva's protection, we will definitely not suffer," Namo Avalokitesvara Bodhisattva, Namo Ksitigarbha Bodhisattva.

The young men shake their heads and walk away, saying: "You rely on the Bodhisattva," sighing, "The harm of superstition, so poisonous, is even more poisonous than poison itself."

As the old woman is chanting to the Bodhisattva, a monk walks in, she hurriedly stands up and says, "Master, please sit," pouring a cup of tea and handing it to the monk.

The monk, smiling, accepts the tea and says: "Good day to you, old lady, it's been a long time since you came to my temple, I've been thinking of you very much, so I came to visit you today."

(Old woman) Thank you, Master, because my daughter-in-law has gone to her parents' home, and it's been several months since she returned. These days I often have headaches, sometimes cold, sometimes hot. I wanted to go to your temple to pray to the Bodhisattva, I don't know if I will die or not?

(Monk) Old lady, you've been sweeping the floor and scrubbing, you must be tired. Tomorrow I will pray to the Great Emperor Bodhisattva for you and bring back some medicinal pills to swallow, you will naturally get better. Your spirit is very good, you will definitely not die, besides, you are fervently devoted to the Bodhisattva, the Bodhisattva will protect you from death.

(Old woman) Ha!! Laughing, she says: "Master, will I really not die? When you pray to the Bodhisattva, please also ask for me, protect me so I can live a few more years, don't forget."

(Monk) I won't forget, now there are many people praying to the Bodhisattva and burning incense in my temple, it's crowded every day. I want to add a rear hall, sculpt a statue of Amitabha Buddha, and build eighteen Arhats on both sides, so I came to discuss it with you, what do you think?

(Old woman) I've long wanted to contribute to the temple, to add a rear hall, but because I haven't had the time, it's been delayed until now. Now that you have already made a vow, that's the best, it should be expanded.

(Monk) I've brought the donation book, I'll leave one with you, please help the Bodhisattva.

(Old woman) This is my duty, come tomorrow and I will write it with you.

"The monk hands a donation book to the old woman."

The old woman looks at it and says: "How can such a thin book be enough to write for our big village? Bring a few more tomorrow. I've already calculated, Mrs. Wang's family two hundred dollars, Grandma Li's is also two hundred dollars, Mrs. Zhang's is also two hundred dollars, and the young lady is one hundred dollars, there are many who will donate several hundred dollars. I myself plan to write three hundred dollars, two hundred dollars written in my own name, and one hundred dollars written anonymously. If my son sees it, more than the other ladies, he will grumble and scold me, I'm informing you in advance."

(Monk) Thank you for the Madam's kindness, for such enthusiasm, most importantly the Bodhisattva will protect you, light feet and healthy hands, I'm leaving, old lady, please sit.

The old woman sends him to the door and says, "Master, please take care on your way."

Mini Biographies of Stars

Garbo's Childhood Realism (Continued) 184

— Yesterday

I told her brother that I found it strange, or at least interesting, that Greta had achieved such fame as an actress.

Her brother, who was seven years older than her, was very handsome, with an endearing manner and speech. Hearing my words, he shook his head, his eyes shining with a strange light, and smiled:

"Yes, I think it's strange." He fiddled with a cigarette in his hand. "But I'm still not surprised. When she was little, she had a kind of magic that made you have to believe. Of course, I'm speaking from the position of her brother. But indeed, her various traits made you have to believe."

"But how did she happen to choose an acting career? Was it accidental, or did she have such an ambition from early on?"

Garbo's brother laughed.

"She often liked acting when she was very young. That's why I say she originally had this ambition."

Then we talked about various careers, about how many people relied on the encouragement of ambition to achieve success. Finally, I talked about his sister's career, and at this time, I felt a humorous sentiment.

"Sometimes it seems strange that she can have the reputation you said she has today, but I still think of her as my little sister; I really find it hard to believe she's a famous person. I feel like she's always been my little sister."

Our conversation was full of a natural sentiment, lovely gestures, and complete understanding. This was mainly because Garbo's brother—his name is Sven, Gustafsson—was a famously interesting person. He married an American woman and had traveled all over the continent, but he still wanted to travel to America.

But all of the above are her brother's words, her own family's words. So I decided to talk to others who knew Garbo as a child. At the house where Garbo was born and grew up, number thirty-two on Brahegatan Street, I spoke with Mrs. Emanuel Long, who remembered this girl named Garbo very well, as she lived next door.

○ ○ ○ ○ ○ ○ ○ ○

Mrs. Long is a short, plump woman, taking care of her sick husband. She lamented her circumstances, but when Garbo's name was mentioned, her light blue eyes shone with joy.

"Yes, I remember her very well."

I asked her a few questions about Garbo's childhood.

Mrs. Long sighed slightly, recalling the past.

"She was always happy, full of energy. She often played in my house, I really liked her, everyone liked her for no reason." Mrs. Long sighed.

"I'm not surprised by her success today, she has the talent to be an actress, because when she was young..." (To be continued)

Sweet Girl Nimka Roh's Halloween Celebration

Rare News From The Film World

Ziegfeld's Posthumous Honors 185

— Zhenhua

Most of Hollywood's stars come from the Ziegfeld Follies, so the film industry values it very highly. The leader of the Follies, Mr. Ziegfeld, recently passed away suddenly due to a serious illness. Therefore, Eddie Cantor, Marion Miller, Mary Tristler, Dolores McQuinn, Will Rogers, Marilyn Davies, LuFanli, Billie Dumey, and many other big stars were very sad upon hearing this bad news.

Ziegfeld's wife, Billie Blank, was filming for RKO Pictures, and was near completion, when she suddenly received the telegram of her husband's death. She was overwhelmed with grief. At the same time, Hollywood stars, for the death of this great musical master, also shed many tears for him.

Contentment Brings No Disgrace 186

— Zhenhua

Everyone thinks it's a laughing matter that Hollywood stars, who make five thousand dollars a week, are still not satisfied and often run away in a huff. Meanwhile, a young star, Robert Young, who is also loved by the audience, receives so many letters every day that two postmen are not enough to deliver them. But he is very content with his salary of two hundred and fifty dollars a week, which supports his family, and he still has to pay sixteen dollars and two cents a month for car expenses.

Overseas News

The Resurgence of "All-Star Casts" 187

— Xing

Hollywood, where new tricks are constantly emerging, is now showing a resurgence of the "all-star cast" format that was previously only occasionally used. Recently, MGM used many stars to co-star in the drama "Grand Hotel" (scheduled to be shown at the Grand Theater in Shanghai on January 1st next year as a big hit), which received unprecedented welcome from the American audience, leading to a major reform in the American film industry. All companies feel that the future of the film industry cannot attract people's attention without this method, so other companies are also trying their best to adopt this method to shoot great films, fortunately, MGM does not have a patent on this method.

The news is that two companies have already mobilized all their forces.

Fox is currently shooting a film called "State Fair," starring Will Rogers, Janet Gaynor, Charles Farrell, Jimmie Dunn, Sally Eilers, etc. Every minor role is not played by "unknown people," and a lot of capital is also used to create magnificent sets and special costumes, with everything that a big production should have.

Paramount also has the most stars, comparable to MGM, so it is easier to shoot this kind of film. They are now preparing a script called "The Big Broadcast," and almost every famous actor in their company is included.

This is generally recognized as a good trend. The American film industry believes that this trend will dominate the entire direction of future films. This is something our movie fans are very happy to know.

Child Stars Active on the Screen 188

— Jizhong

Several years ago, domestic films starring child stars were quite numerous, with Erchun, Ren Chaojun, Gu Baolian, Chen Shaoyu, etc., being the most notable. However, because the authorities did not pay attention to them, children's films disappeared from the silver screen. Compared to the attention paid to the naive performances of child stars in imported films, the difference is immeasurable.

Now, because the child stars in Lianhua's "Humanity" and Tianyi's "One Night of Luxury" are so popular, the domestic film industry is paying attention to this matter again. First, there was Li Keng starring in "Childhood China," and then Yuan Meiyun starring in "Little Actress." Now news comes that Moonbright Company, which specializes in martial arts films, is also starring two films by Ren Pengnian and Lao Guan's daughter, Xiao Wumo Zhu, named "Her Heart" and "Blood Letter." At the same time, Gu Baolian will also return to the screen, starring in a sound film for Huaguang.

Will child stars once again be active on the screen?

Anecdotes

Elegant Affairs of Talented People 189

— He

Clive Brook recently prepared an epitaph, intending to place it in front of his grave after his death, which reads, "Please forgive me for not being able to stand up and greet you." How humorous that is!

Where is the Wealthy Star? 190

— He

The handsome Rudolph Valentino once went to pick up a newly made suit, using one-third of the money he earned from a film shoot to pay the famous Hollywood tailor as a small deposit, but the tailor refused.

Prematurely Gray Hair 191

— He

Billie Dove's hair turned gray very early. According to her, it gradually became like this from the age of thirteen.

Dislocated Neck Upon Entering the Scene 192

—

Colleen Moore, when she first entered the film industry, encountered an unfortunate event while filming, which was dislocating her neck. She still tells everyone about it to this day!

The Only Reservation 193

— He

Andy Clyde's contract with his company stipulated that "under no circumstances shall the company ask him to shave off his mustache."

New Film Introductions

1) Spring Breeze, Willows 194

— Jizhong

"Spring Breeze, Willows" is the maiden work of Wang Fuqing's personally and painstakingly managed Great East Golden Lion Company. This sound film does not borrow any external forces, and is entirely the result of Li Qingxian's private research and success. This is something that deserves our attention.

This commercial film is directed by Wang Fuqing himself. The leading roles are played by Yang Naimei, Chen Yitang, Xia Peizhen, Hu Jia, etc. Judging from their past honors, this time should not disappoint us.

2) Struggle 195

"Struggle" is a film produced by Lianhua's second production studio, directed by Shi Dongshan, his first work after changing his style. The main actors are Chen Yanyan, Zheng Junli, Yuan Congmei, etc. The plot is close to a humorous and realistic style, full of an energetic new spirit, and will be released at the Beijing Grand Theater this month.

Basic Film Knowledge 196

— Yuxiang

Watching movies is a very common thing, but there are many things that are worth our attention. I will list a few below for your reference.

1. Regularly read various reports about movies to know the news of new films and see people's reviews of new films, so you won't be fooled by worthless films.

2. Some theaters allow you to reserve seats, so it's best to reserve in advance to avoid temporary crowding.

3. Some theaters allow you to buy bulk tickets, but don't be greedy for small gains, because these bulk tickets are often invalid when good movies are playing.

4. It's best not to bring children under two or four years old to see a movie, to avoid them crying during the performance and disturbing others.

5. Before the show starts, it's best to read the synopsis to know the general plot of the movie.

6. When watching a movie, if two people go together, don't talk or clap your hands when the performance is exciting, because these bad habits often lower your personality, especially in high-end theaters.

7. If you are wearing a hat, it is best to take it off and put it on your lap to avoid obstructing other people's vision, but do not put it on the hat hook under the seat, because it is often stolen.

8. It is often very expensive to take a rickshaw when leaving, so it is better to walk a few steps and sit further away from the theater.

John Gilbert's Fourth Wedding 197

— Jianan

We imagine that the wedding ceremonies of Hollywood stars, who live a luxurious life, must be very extravagant and lively. But Gilbert's wedding this time—his fourth—is surprising.

On the evening of the wedding date, the bride, Virginia Bruce, quietly returned from the set, wiped off the greasepaint, took off her makeup, put on a black crepe dress with light sleeves, and slowly ran to a quiet hut, where she completed the marriage ceremony with Gilbert.

Besides the bridesmaids and Norma Shearer, there were very few other guests present. And early the next morning, the bride was busy continuing her work filming "Kongo," with no plans for a honeymoon.

Film Studies

Attractive Eyes 198

People with great ambition and courage like to look into the pupils of other people's eyes, while people who are timid and weak easily avoid such gazes. When experienced directors hire new actors, they can determine whether a person can act or not with just a glance at the initial meeting. Experienced doctors or astrologers, upon meeting someone, look straight into their eyes, seeing all the way into their heart, and then state the results of their observation. When hypnotists perform hypnosis, their pair of magical eyes shine straight into your pupils, and your spirit is naturally and inevitably subdued by them.

Whether eyes are powerful or not has a great relationship even with ordinary people, let alone those of us whose profession is to express hypothetical situations? Ordinary people with a little experience in social interaction understand the necessity of training their eyes, often intentionally or unintentionally training them when grooming, let alone us, can we not think of a way to hone them day and night?

The more you train your eyes, the stronger they become. A pair of naturally attractive eyes is certainly the greatest happiness in your life, but without honing, you still cannot achieve satisfactory results. What is the difference between angry eyes and panicked eyes? You are naturally very skilled at dealing with real environments; angry eyes have their own look, and panicked eyes have their own look. But what about when you're on set? American photographers, even when filming famous stars, sometimes find that the angry eyes in a certain shot look a bit like fearful eyes, and so they have to ask the entire cast to reshoot that shot.
